## Instruction

Today we have 3 new employees joining us, and each employee's information is stored in the Snowflake database.

Based on the employee's group assignment and training manual, automatically generate training task lists, send emails to the employee's email address, and update the task content and planned completion dates to the database.

For new employees, send onboarding emails in the following format:

```
Dear xxx, You have the following training tasks to complete:
xxx
xxx
xxx
Please complete them as soon as possible.
```

Additionally, you need to check for employee records where the current date has exceeded the training completion deadline but the task status is still "incomplete", send reminder emails to the employees themselves in the same format.

The order of the tasks in the email should be based on the order in the training manual.

And remember to CC their direct supervisor.

## Initial State

### Snowflake

You can view the database build process [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/landing-task-reminder/preprocess).

```json
	"query": "-- Find overdue public tasks\nSELECT \n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n    e.NAME,
	 \n    e.EMAIL,
	 \n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,

	 \n    pt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 pt.DDL,
	 '2025-09-21') as DAYS_OVERDUE\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.PUBLIC_TASKS pt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON pt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE pt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \nAND pt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\nORDER BY e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 pt.DDL"
```

```json
{
	"query": "-- Find overdue group tasks from all groups\nSELECT \n    'BACKEND' as GROUP_NAME,
	\n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n    e.NAME,
	 \n    e.EMAIL,
	 \n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    gt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n    gt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 gt.DDL,
	 '2025-09-21') as DAYS_OVERDUE\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND gt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE gt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \nAND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n\nUNION ALL\n\nSELECT \n    'FRONTEND' as GROUP_NAME,
	\n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n    e.NAME,
	 \n    e.EMAIL,
	 \n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    gt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n    gt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 gt.DDL,
	 '2025-09-21') as DAYS_OVERDUE\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND gt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE gt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \nAND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n\nUNION ALL\n\nSELECT \n    'TESTING' as GROUP_NAME,
	\n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n    e.NAME,
	 \n    e.EMAIL,
	 \n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    gt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n    gt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 gt.DDL,
	 '2025-09-21') as DAYS_OVERDUE\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING gt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE gt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \nAND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n\nUNION ALL\n\nSELECT \n    'DATA' as GROUP_NAME,
	\n    e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n    e.NAME,
	 \n    e.EMAIL,
	 \n    e.REPORT_TO_ID,
	\n    sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    gt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n    gt.DDL,
	\n    DATEDIFF(day,
	 gt.DDL,
	 '2025-09-21') as DAYS_OVERDUE\nFROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_DATA gt\nJOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\nLEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\nWHERE gt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \nAND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n\nORDER BY EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 DDL"
}
```

```json
{
	"query": "-- Get all overdue tasks grouped by employee\nWITH overdue_public AS (\n    SELECT \n        e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n        e.NAME,
	 \n        e.EMAIL,
	 \n        sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n        pt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n        pt.DDL\n    FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.PUBLIC_TASKS pt\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON pt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    LEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    WHERE pt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \n    AND pt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n),
	\noverdue_group AS (\n    SELECT \n        e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n        e.NAME,
	 \n        e.EMAIL,
	 \n        sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n        gt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n        gt.DDL\n    FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_BACKEND gt\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    LEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    WHERE gt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \n    AND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n    \n    UNION ALL\n    \n    SELECT \n        e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n        e.NAME,
	 \n        e.EMAIL,
	 \n        sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n        gt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n        gt.DDL\n    FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_FRONTEND gt\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    LEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    WHERE gt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \n    AND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n    \n    UNION ALL\n    \n    SELECT \n        e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n        e.NAME,
	 \n        e.EMAIL,
	 \n        sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n        gt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n        gt.DDL\n    FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_TESTING gt\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    LEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    WHERE gt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \n    AND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n    \n    UNION ALL\n    \n    SELECT \n        e.EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 \n        e.NAME,
	 \n        e.EMAIL,
	 \n        sup.EMAIL as SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n        gt.TASK_NAME,
	 \n        gt.DDL\n    FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.GROUP_TASKS_DATA gt\n    JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE e ON gt.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    LEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE sup ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = sup.EMPLOYEE_ID\n    WHERE gt.DDL < '2025-09-21' \n    AND gt.FINISHED_FLAG = false\n),
	\nall_overdue AS (\n    SELECT * FROM overdue_public\n    UNION ALL\n    SELECT * FROM overdue_group\n)\nSELECT \n    EMPLOYEE_ID,
	\n    NAME,
	\n    EMAIL,
	\n    SUPERVISOR_EMAIL,
	\n    LISTAGG(TASK_NAME || ' (Due: ' || DDL || ')',
	 '\\n') WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY DDL) as OVERDUE_TASKS\nFROM all_overdue\nGROUP BY EMPLOYEE_ID,
	 NAME,
	 EMAIL,
	 SUPERVISOR_EMAIL\nORDER BY EMPLOYEE_ID"
}
```
</div>

```json
{
```
```json
	"query":"SELECT e.NAME,
	 e.EMAIL,
```
```json
	 t.TASK_NAME,
	 t.DDL,
	 s.EMAIL AS SUPERVISOR_EMAIL FROM LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.PUBLIC_TASKS AS t JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE AS e ON t.EMPLOYEE_ID = e.EMPLOYEE_ID LEFT JOIN LANDING_TASK_REMINDER.PUBLIC.EMPLOYEE AS s ON e.REPORT_TO_ID = s.EMPLOYEE_ID WHERE t.DDL < '2025-10-21' AND t.FINISHED_FLAG = FALSE"
}
```
